// @public
export interface DefinedSchema<TProperties extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder> = Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> {
    create(properties: InferCreateProps<TProperties>, options: CreateNodeOptions): InferNode<TProperties>;
    is(node: Node_2): node is InferNode<TProperties>;
    readonly _properties: TProperties;
    schema: Schema;
    readonly _schemaId: SchemaIRI;
    validate(node: unknown): ValidationResult;
}

// @public
export interface DefineSchemaOptions<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder>, A extends AuthorizationDefinition = AuthorizationDefinition> {
    authorization?: A;
    // Warning: (ae-forgotten-export) The symbol "DocumentType_2" needs to be exported by the entry point index.d.ts
    document?: DocumentType_2;
    extends?: DefinedSchema<Record<string, PropertyBuilder>>;
    migrateFrom?: SchemaIRI;
    name: string;
    namespace: `xnet://${string}/`;
    properties: P;
    version?: string;
}

// @public (undocumented)

    allowed: true;
    provider: ExternalReferenceProvider;
    embedUrl: string;
    origin: string;
    sandbox: string;
    allow: string;
    referrerPolicy: ReferrerPolicy;
} | {
    allowed: false;
    provider: ExternalReferenceProvider;
    embedUrl: string | null;
    origin: string | null;
    reason: ExternalReferenceEmbedBlockReason;
};

// Warning: (ae-forgotten-export) The symbol "RequiredKeys" needs to be exported by the entry point index.d.ts
// Warning: (ae-forgotten-export) The symbol "OptionalKeys" needs to be exported by the entry point index.d.ts
//
// @public
export type InferCreateProps<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> = {
    [K in RequiredKeys<P>]: InferPropertyType<P[K]>;
} & {
    [K in OptionalKeys<P>]?: InferPropertyType<P[K]> | undefined;
};

// @public
export type InferNode<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> = {
    id: string;
    schemaId: SchemaIRI;
    createdAt: number;
    createdBy: DID;
} & InferProperties<P>;

// @public
export type InferProperties<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> = {
    [K in RequiredKeys<P>]: InferPropertyType<P[K]>;
} & {
    [K in OptionalKeys<P>]?: InferPropertyType<P[K]>;
};

// @public
export type InferPropertyType<B> = B extends PropertyBuilder<infer T> ? T : never;

// @public

    name: string;
    sampleValues?: unknown[];
    type: ColumnType;
}

    register(lens: SchemaLens): void;
    transform(data: Record<string, unknown>, from: SchemaIRI, to: SchemaIRI): Record<string, unknown>;
    transformWithDetails(data: Record<string, unknown>, from: SchemaIRI, to: SchemaIRI): MigrationResult;
    unregister(source: SchemaIRI, target: SchemaIRI): boolean;
}

    // (undocumented)

// @public (undocumented)
export interface NodeQueryOptions<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder> = Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> {
    // (undocumented)
    includeDeleted?: boolean;
    // (undocumented)
    limit?: number;
    // (undocumented)
    materializedView?: string | NodeQueryMaterializedViewOptions;
    // (undocumented)
    nodeId?: string;
    // (undocumented)
    offset?: number;
    // (undocumented)
    orderBy?: {
        [K in keyof InferCreateProps<P> | SystemOrderField]?: SortDirection;
    };
    // (undocumented)
    page?: NodeQueryPageOptions;
    // (undocumented)
    search?: string | NodeQuerySearchFilter;
    // (undocumented)
    spatial?: NodeQuerySpatialFilter;
    // (undocumented)
    where?: Partial<InferCreateProps<P>>;
}

// @public
export interface NodeStoreOptions {
    auth?: StoreAuthAPI;
    authEvaluator?: PolicyEvaluator;
    authorDID: DID_2;
    authRelevantPropertyLookup?: (schemaId: SchemaIRI) => Set<string> | undefined;
    changeSigner?: ChangeSigner;
    contentKeyCache?: ContentKeyCache;
    lensRegistry?: LensRegistry;
    nodeContentCipher?: NodeContentCipher;
    onRecipientsMayNeedRecompute?: (context: {
        nodeId: NodeId;
        schemaId: SchemaIRI;
        changedProperties: string[];
    }) => Promise<void> | void;
    onUnauthorizedRemoteChange?: (context: {
        change: NodeChange;
        action: AuthAction;
        decision: AuthDecision;
    }) => void;
    // Warning: (ae-forgotten-export) The symbol "PropertyLookup" needs to be exported by the entry point index.d.ts
    propertyLookup?: PropertyLookup;
    schemaLookup?: SchemaLookup;
    signingKey: Uint8Array;
    storage: NodeStorageAdapter;
    telemetry?: {
        reportPerformance(metricName: string, durationMs: number, codeNamespace?: string): void;
        reportUsage(metricName: string, value: number): void;
        reportCrash(error: Error, context?: {
            codeNamespace?: string;
        }): void;
        reportSecurityEvent(eventName: string, severity: 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' | 'critical'): void;
    };
}

// @public
export interface PropertyBuilder<T = unknown> {
    coerce(value: unknown): T | null;
    definition: Omit<PropertyDefinition_2, '@id' | 'name'>;
    _type: T;
    validate(value: unknown): value is T;
}

// @public
interface PropertyDefinition_2 {
    '@id': string;
    config?: Record<string, unknown>;
    name: string;
    readonly?: boolean;
    required: boolean;
    type: PropertyType;
}
export { PropertyDefinition_2 as PropertyDefinition }

// @public
export const QUERY_AST_VERSION: 1;

// @public
export interface QueryableRow extends FilterableRow, SortableRow, GroupableRow {
    // (undocumented)
    cells: Record<string, unknown>;
    // (undocumented)
    id: string;
    // (undocumented)

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryAST = QueryASTNodeQuery | QueryASTQuerySet;

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTAggregate = {
    kind: 'aggregate';
    alias: string;
    function: QueryASTAggregateFunction;
    field?: string;
    groupBy?: string[];
    having?: QueryASTPredicate;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTAggregateExecution = {
    scope: 'loaded-snapshot';
    rowCount: number;
    results: Record<string, QueryASTAggregateResult>;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTAggregateFunction = 'count' | 'countDistinct' | 'sum' | 'avg' | 'min' | 'max';

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTAggregateGroup = {
    key: Record<string, unknown>;
    rowCount: number;
    value: unknown;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTAggregatePlan = {
    path: string;
    alias: string;
    function: QueryASTAggregateFunction;
    strategy: 'node-count' | 'scalar-scan' | 'distinct-scan';
    requiredFields: string[];
    groupBy: string[];
    canUseScalarIndex: boolean;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTAggregateResult = {
    alias: string;
    function: QueryASTAggregateFunction;
    field?: string;
    groupBy: string[];
    rowCount: number;
    value: unknown;
    groups?: QueryASTAggregateGroup[];
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTComparisonPredicate = {
    kind: 'comparison';
    field: string;
    op: QueryASTOperator;
    value?: unknown;
    values?: unknown[];
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTCompoundPredicate = {
    kind: 'and' | 'or';
    predicates: QueryASTPredicate[];
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTField<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder> = Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> = Extract<keyof InferCreateProps<P>, string>;

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTIncludes = Record<string, QueryASTRelationInclude>;

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTNodeQuery = {
    version: QueryASTVersion;
    kind: 'node';
    schemaId: SchemaIRI;
    predicate?: QueryASTPredicate;
    orderBy?: QueryASTOrderBy[];
    page?: QueryASTPage;
    include?: QueryASTIncludes;
    aggregates?: QueryASTAggregate[];
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTNodeQueryOptions<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder> = Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> = {
    where?: QueryASTPredicate | QueryASTPredicate[];
    orderBy?: Partial<Record<QueryASTField<P> | SystemOrderField, SortDirection>>;
    page?: QueryASTPage;
    include?: QueryASTIncludes;
    aggregates?: QueryASTAggregate[];
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTNotPredicate = {
    kind: 'not';
    predicate: QueryASTPredicate;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTOperator = 'eq' | 'neq' | 'gt' | 'gte' | 'lt' | 'lte' | 'between' | 'in' | 'contains' | 'startsWith' | 'isNull' | 'isNotNull';

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTOrderBy = {
    field: string;
    direction: SortDirection;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTPage = {
    first?: number;
    after?: string;
    offset?: number;
    count?: NodeQueryPageCountMode;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTPlannerGate = {
    validation: QueryASTValidationResult;
    relationIndexRequirements: QueryASTRelationIndexRequirement[];
    aggregatePlans: QueryASTAggregatePlan[];
    useFindReady: boolean;
    blockers: string[];
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTPredicate = QueryASTComparisonPredicate | QueryASTCompoundPredicate | QueryASTNotPredicate;

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTQuerySet = {
    version: QueryASTVersion;
    kind: 'query-set';
    mode: 'batch' | 'dashboard';
    queries: Record<string, QueryASTNodeQuery>;
    aggregates?: QueryASTQuerySetAggregate[];
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTQuerySetAggregate = {
    kind: 'query-set-aggregate';
    alias: string;
    query: string;
    function: QueryASTAggregateFunction;
    field?: string;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTRelationDirection = 'outbound' | 'inbound';

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTRelationInclude = {
    kind: 'relation-include';
    direction: QueryASTRelationDirection;
    field: string;
    targetSchemaId: SchemaIRI;
    query: QueryASTNodeQuery;
    cardinality: 'one' | 'many';
    required?: boolean;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTRelationIncludeOptions<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder> = Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> = QueryASTNodeQueryOptions<P> & {
    cardinality?: 'one' | 'many';
    required?: boolean;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTRelationIndexRequirement = {
    schemaId: SchemaIRI;
    property: string;
    direction: QueryASTRelationDirection;
    targetSchemaId: SchemaIRI;
    reason: 'include';
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTSchemaInput<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder> = Record<string, PropertyBuilder>> = SchemaIRI | DefinedSchema<P>;

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTValidationError = {
    path: string;
    code: string;
    message: string;
    value?: unknown;
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTValidationResult = {
    valid: boolean;
    errors: QueryASTValidationError[];
};

// @public (undocumented)
export type QueryASTVersion = typeof QUERY_AST_VERSION;

// @public (undocumented)
export function queryOperators<P extends Record<string, PropertyBuilder>>(): {
    eq: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, value: InferCreateProps<P>[K]) => QueryASTPredicate;
    neq: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, value: InferCreateProps<P>[K]) => QueryASTPredicate;
    gt: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, value: InferCreateProps<P>[K]) => QueryASTPredicate;
    gte: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, value: InferCreateProps<P>[K]) => QueryASTPredicate;
    lt: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, value: InferCreateProps<P>[K]) => QueryASTPredicate;
    lte: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, value: InferCreateProps<P>[K]) => QueryASTPredicate;
    between: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, from: InferCreateProps<P>[K], to: InferCreateProps<P>[K]) => QueryASTPredicate;
    includesAny: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, values: InferCreateProps<P>[K][]) => QueryASTPredicate;
    contains: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, value: string) => QueryASTPredicate;
    startsWith: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K, value: string) => QueryASTPredicate;
    isNull: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K) => QueryASTPredicate;
    isNotNull: <K extends QueryASTField<P>>(field: K) => QueryASTPredicate;
};

}

    groups: RowGroup<T>[];
    total: number;
}

    getNodes(ids: readonly NodeId[]): Promise<NodeState[]>;

    // (undocumented)
    getSQLiteAdapter(): SQLiteAdapter;

    getSyncCursor(room: string): Promise<number>;

        nodeId: NodeId;

        deleted: number;
    }>;

    queryNodes(descriptor: NodeQueryDescriptor): Promise<NodeQueryResult>;

        nodeId: string;

        node?: {
            schemaId: SchemaIRI;
            createdBy?: DID_2;
            properties?: Record<string, unknown>;
        };
    }): Promise<AuthDecision>;
    // (undocumented)
    explain(input: {
        action: AuthAction;
        nodeId: string;
    }): Promise<AuthTrace>;
    // (undocumented)
    getOfflinePolicy(): OfflineAuthPolicy;
    // (undocumented)
    grant(input: GrantInput): Promise<AuthGrant>;
    // (undocumented)
    listGrants(input: {
        nodeId: string;
        status?: GrantStatus;
    }): Promise<AuthGrant[]>;
    // (undocumented)
    listIssuedGrants(): Promise<AuthGrant[]>;
    // (undocumented)
    listReceivedGrants(): Promise<AuthGrant[]>;
    // (undocumented)
    revoke(input: {
        grantId: string;
    }): Promise<void>;
    // (undocumented)
    setOfflinePolicy(policy: Partial<OfflineAuthPolicy>): void;
}
